         <h1 id="gitlab-docs">GitLab Docs<a href="#gitlab-docs" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h1> 
         <p>Welcome to <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/">GitLab</a> documentation. </p>
         <p>Here you can access the complete documentation for GitLab, the single application for the <a href="#the-entire-devops-lifecycle">entire DevOps lifecycle</a>. </p>
         <h2 id="overview">Overview<a href="#overview" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>No matter how you use GitLab, we have documentation for you. </p>
         <table>

         <h2 id="the-entire-devops-lifecycle">The entire DevOps lifecycle<a href="#the-entire-devops-lifecycle" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>GitLab is the first single application for software development, security, and operations that enables <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/topics/concurrent-devops/">Concurrent DevOps</a>. GitLab makes the software lifecycle faster and radically improves the speed of business. </p>
         <p>GitLab provides solutions for <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/stages-devops-lifecycle/">each of the stages of the DevOps lifecycle</a>. </p>
         <h2 id="new-to-git-and-gitlab">New to Git and GitLab?<a href="#new-to-git-and-gitlab" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>Working with new systems can be daunting. </p>
         <p>We have the following documentation to rapidly uplift your GitLab knowledge: </p>
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th style="text-align:left">Topic </th>
            <th style="text-align:left">Description </th>
           </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="gitlab-basics/index.html">GitLab basics guides</a> </td>
            <td style="text-align:left">Start working on the command line and with GitLab. </td>
           </tr>
           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="https://about.gitlab.com/topics/version-control/what-is-gitlab-workflow/">GitLab workflow overview</a> </td>
            <td style="text-align:left">Enhance your workflow with the best of GitLab Workflow. </td>
           </tr>
           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="ci/quick_start/index.html">Get started with GitLab CI/CD</a> </td>
            <td style="text-align:left">Quickly implement GitLab CI/CD. </td>
           </tr>
           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="topics/autodevops/index.html">Auto DevOps</a> </td>

           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="user/markdown.html">GitLab Markdown</a> </td>

          </tbody>

         <h2 id="contributing-to-gitlab">Contributing to GitLab<a href="#contributing-to-gitlab" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>GitLab Community Edition is <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab-foss/">open source</a> and GitLab Enterprise Edition is <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab/">open-core</a>. </p>
         <p>Learn how to contribute to GitLab with the following resources: </p>
         <table> 
          <thead>

            <th style="text-align:left">Description </th>

           </tr>
           <tr> 
            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="legal/index.html">Legal</a> </td>

            <td style="text-align:left"><a href="development/documentation/index.html">Writing documentation</a> </td>
            <td style="text-align:left">How to contribute to GitLab Docs. </td>
